***четверть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:четверть.html>че́тверть</a> (3062)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:четверть.html>че́тверть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čétvertʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:четверть.html>че́тверти</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:четверть.html>че́тверти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:четверть.html>четверте́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>quarter, fourth, quadrant
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:четверть.html>че́тверть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:второй.html>второ́го</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čétvertʹ</b> vtoróvo</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>quarter</b> past one (<i>time</i>)</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:четверть.html>че́тверти</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bez <b>čétverti</b> dva</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>quarter</b> to two (<i>time</i>)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>school term, quarter</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">astronomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> quarter, crescent (phase of the moon)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> crotchet, quarter note, fourth note (musical note)</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">четвертовать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">četvertovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:чет.html>че́т</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>верть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 3-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 8e  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-чет-</b>; интерфикс: <b>-в-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ерть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:четкий.html>чётки</a> (20631)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9a/Tespih_fcm.jpg/220px-Tespih_fcm.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="434" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9a/Tespih_fcm.jpg/330px-Tespih_fcm.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9a/Tespih_fcm.jpg/440px-Tespih_fcm.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1152" data-file-height="2273" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:четкий.html>чётки</a></div></div></div>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:четкий.html>чётки</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čótki</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:четкий.html>чёток</a></b>, <i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>Orthodox Prayer Rope</li>
<li>rosary, prayer beads, paternoster (Catholic prayer beads)</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:четкий.html>чёткий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čótkij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)чётче</b>)

***четкость.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:четкость.html>чёткость</a> (16005)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:четкий.html>чёткий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čótkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:четкость.html>чёткость</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čótkostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:четкость.html>чёткости</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>clearness, legibility
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:четкость.html>чёткость</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:изображение.html>изображе́ния</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čótkostʹ</b> izobražénija</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">image definition quality</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:телевидение.html>телеви́дение</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:высокий.html>высо́кой</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:четкость.html>чёткости</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">televídenije vysókoj <b>čótkosti</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">high-definition television</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>accuracy, precision, preciseness, efficiency</li></ol>

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-четыр-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-е</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***четыреста.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:четыреста.html>четы́реста</a> (7158)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:четыреста.html>четы́реста</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">četýresta</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>four hundred (400)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><b><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:четыреста.html>четы́реста</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">četýresta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></b> in the nominative case governs the genitive plural of the noun.
</p>
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:четыреста.html>четы́реста</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>četýresta</b> málʹčikov</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>four hundred</b> boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:четыреста.html>четы́реста</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">málʹčikov <b>četýresta</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">approximately <b>four hundred</b> boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:четыреста.html>четы́реста</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́г</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>četýresta</b> knig</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>four hundred</b> books</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>они́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́х</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:четыреста.html>четырёхста́х</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:солдат.html>солда́тах</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oní govoríli o svoíx <b>četyrjoxstáx</b> soldátax.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">They were talking about their <b>four hundred</b> soldiers.</span></div></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">четырёхсотле́тие</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">četyrjoxsotlétije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***четырнадцать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:четырнадцать.html>четы́рнадцать</a> (5424)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compounded from <b><a href = vnd.unilang:четыре.html>четы́ре</a></b> + <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> + <b>дцать</b>, or <i>four on ten</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:четырнадцать.html>четы́рнадцать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">četýrnadcatʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>fourteen (14)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:четырнадцать.html>четы́рнадцать</a></strong></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">četyrnadcatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in the nominative case and accusative case governs the genitive plural of the noun. In other cases, it governs the corresponding plural case of the noun.
</p>
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:четырнадцать.html>четы́рнадцать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>četýrnadcatʹ</b> málʹčikov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fourteen boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:четырнадцать.html>четы́рнадцатью</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиками</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>četýrnadcatʹju</b> málʹčikami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">with fourteen boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:четырнадцать.html>четы́рнадцать</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">málʹčikov <b>četýrnadcatʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">approximately fourteen boys</span></div></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>че<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ты́р<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>над</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>цать</b>
</p><p>Числительное, <a href = vnd.unilang:количественный.html>коли́чественное</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:порядковый.html>поря́дковое</a> числительное — <a href = vnd.unilang:четырнадцатый.html>четы́рнадцатый</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-четыр-</b>; суффикс: <b>-надцать</b>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чех.html>чех</a> (5860)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">Čech</i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чех.html>чех</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čex</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чех.html>че́ха</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чех.html>че́хи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чех.html>че́хов</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">че́шка</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>male Czech (person)</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms_2">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чеченец.html>чече́нец</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">čečénec</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a Chechen man</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which has a similar sound, but has nothing to do with the Czech people.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чех.html>чех</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čex</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чех.html>че́ха</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чех.html>че́хи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чех.html>че́хов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang<span class="ib-comma">,</span> rare</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a Chechen man, especially during the two Chechen conflicts</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">чехолъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čexolŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">чехълъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čexŭlŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čexъlъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1c  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> знач. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицо́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:занимающий.html>занима́ющее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:должность.html>до́лжность</a>,</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склоняться.html>склоня́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:образец.html>образцу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>существи́тельных</a> (<span title="в винительном падеже"><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кого́</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a>?</span> — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:чин.html>чи́на</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:чин.html>чино́в</a></i>).

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чинить.html>чини́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">činítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:починить.html>почини́ть</a></b>)

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чинить.html>чини́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">činítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учинить.html>учини́ть</a></b>)

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>чи<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:нить.html>ни́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c(4).      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:починить.html>почини́ть</a> (знач. 1); очинить, зачинить (знач. 2).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-чин-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>.
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чинный.html>чи́нный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čínnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чинно.html>чи́нно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čínno</span>)
</p>

<p><b>чи<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́в</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>чий</b>

***чирикать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чирикать.html>чири́кать</a> (24150)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чирикать.html>чири́кать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čiríkatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">чири́кнуть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to chirp, to twitter</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
